<li id="cite_note-rustextofdecl-198"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-rustextofdecl_198-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation news"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://mospat.ru/ru/2016/02/13/news128178/"><bdi lang="ru">Совместное заявление Папы Римского Франциска и Патриарха Московского и всея Руси Кирилла</bdi></a> (in Russian). The official web site of the Moscow Patriarchate. 13 February 2016. <q>§25. Надеемся, что наша встреча внесет вклад в примирение там, где существуют трения между греко-католиками и православными. Сегодня очевидно, что метод "униатизма" прежних веков, предполагающий приведение одной общины в единство с другой путем ее отрыва от своей Церкви, не является путем к восстановлению единства. В то же время, церковные общины, которые появились в результате исторических обстоятельств, имеют право существовать и предпринимать все необходимое для удовлетворения духовных нужд своих верных, стремясь к миру с соседями. Православные и греко-католики нуждаются в примирении и нахождении взаимоприемлемых форм сосуществования.</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.atitle=%D0%A1%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%BC%D0%B5%D1%81%D1%82%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B5+%D0%B7%D0%B0%D1%8F%D0%B2%D0%BB%D0%B5%D0%BD%D0%B8%D0%B5+%D0%9F%D0%B0%D0%BF%D1%8B+%D0%A0%D0%B8%D0%BC%D1%81%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%B3%D0%BE+%D0%A4%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%BD%D1%86%D0%B8%D1%81%D0%BA%D0%B0+%D0%B8+%D0%9F%D0%B0%D1%82%D1%80%D0%B8%D0%B0%D1%80%D1%85%D0%B0+%D0%9C%D0%BE%D1%81%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%B2%D1%81%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%B3%D0%BE+%D0%B8+%D0%B2%D1%81%D0%B5%D1%8F+%D0%A0%D1%83%D1%81%D0%B8+%D0%9A%D0%B8%D1%80%D0%B8%D0%BB%D0%BB%D0%B0&amp;rft.date=2016-02-13&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fmospat.ru%2Fru%2F2016%2F02%2F13%2Fnews128178%2F&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEast%E2%80%93West+Schism" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-alfeevinterv-199"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-alfeevinterv_199-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation news"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://kommersant.ru/doc/2913683"><bdi lang="ru">"Противоречия полностью не преодолены":Глава церковного МИДа митрополит Иларион об отношениях между Московским патриархатом и Ватиканом</bdi></a> (in Russian). <a href="/wiki/Kommersant" title="Kommersant">Kommersant</a>. 11 February 2016. <q>Во-первых, не преодолены вероучительные разногласия. Однако целью встречи и не является обсуждение вероучительных вопросов. Во-вторых, не преодолены те разногласия практического характера, которые омрачают жизнь наших церквей. Я имею в виду прежде всего проблему украинской унии. Разгром униатами трех епархий Московского патриархата в Западной Украине на рубеже 1980–90-х годов, перенос центра Украинской греко-католической церкви из Львова в Киев, настойчивое желание этой церкви присвоить себе статус патриархата, распространение миссии УГКЦ на традиционно православные земли Восточной и Южной Украины, поддержка униатами раскольников – все эти факторы лишь усугубили проблему. Положение еще ухудшилось в результате событий последнего времени на Украине, в которых представители УГКЦ принимали самое непосредственное участие, выступая с антироссийскими и русофобскими лозунгами.</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.atitle=%22%D0%9F%D1%80%D0%BE%D1%82%D0%B8%D0%B2%D0%BE%D1%80%D0%B5%D1%87%D0%B8%D1%8F+%D0%BF%D0%BE%D0%BB%D0%BD%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D1%8C%D1%8E+%D0%BD%D0%B5+%D0%BF%D1%80%D0%B5%D0%BE%D0%B4%D0%BE%D0%BB%D0%B5%D0%BD%D1%8B%22%3A%D0%93%D0%BB%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%B0+%D1%86%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B3%D0%BE+%D0%9C%D0%98%D0%94%D0%B0+%D0%BC%D0%B8%D1%82%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%BF%D0%BE%D0%BB%D0%B8%D1%82+%D0%98%D0%BB%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%B8%D0%BE%D0%BD+%D0%BE%D0%B1+%D0%BE%D1%82%D0%BD%D0%BE%D1%88%D0%B5%D0%BD%D0%B8%D1%8F%D1%85+%D0%BC%D0%B5%D0%B6%D0%B4%D1%83+%D0%9C%D0%BE%D1%81%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%B2%D1%81%D0%BA%D0%B8%D0%BC+%D0%BF%D0%B0%D1%82%D1%80%D0%B8%D0%B0%D1%80%D1%85%D0%B0%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BC+%D0%B8+%D0%92%D0%B0%D1%82%D0%B8%D0%BA%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%BC&amp;rft.date=2016-02-11&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fkommersant.ru%2Fdoc%2F2913683&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEast%E2%80%93West+Schism" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>

<li id="cite_note-217"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-217">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation web">Emmanuel Clapsis. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20080617082301/http://www.goarch.org/en/ourfaith/articles/article8523.asp">"Papal primacy"</a>. Greek Orthodox Archdiocese of America. Archived from <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.goarch.org/en/ourfaith/articles/article8523.asp">the original</a> on 17 June 2008<span class="reference-accessdate">. Retrieved <span class="nowrap">16 October</span> 2008</span>. <q>The regional primacy can be conceived not as power or jurisdiction but only as an expression of the unity and unanimity of all the bishops, and consequently of all the churches, of an area. We must understand the universal primacy of the Roman Church similarly. Based on Christian Tradition, it is possible to affirm the validity of the church of Rome's claims of universal primacy. [...] Orthodoxy does not reject Roman primacy as such, but simply a particular way of understanding that primacy. Within a reintegrated Christendom the bishop of Rome will be considered <i>primus inter pares</i> serving the unity of God's Church in love. He cannot be accepted as set <i>up over</i> the Church as a ruler whose <i>diakonia</i> is conceived through legalistic categories of power of jurisdiction.</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Papal+primacy&amp;rft.pub=Greek+Orthodox+Archdiocese+of+America&amp;rft.au=Emmanuel+Clapsis&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.goarch.org%2Fen%2Fourfaith%2Farticles%2Farticle8523.asp&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEast%E2%80%93West+Schism" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>

<li id="cite_note-240"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-240">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">Lossky, Nikolai. <i>History of Russian Philosophy</i>. p.&#160;87. <a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-0-8236-8074-0" title="Special:BookSources/978-0-8236-8074-0"><bdi>978-0-8236-8074-0</bdi></a>. <q>The legal formalism and logical rationalism of the Catholic Church have their roots in the Roman State. These features developed in it more strongly than ever when the Western Church without consent of the Eastern introduced into the Nicean Creed the filioque clause. Such arbitrary change of the creed is an expression of pride and lack of love for one's brethren in the faith. "In order not to be regarded as a schism by the Church, Romanism was forced to ascribe to the bishop of Rome absolute infallibility." In this way Catholicism broke away from the Church as a whole and became an organization based upon external authority. Its unity is similar to the unity of the state: it is not super-rational but rationalistic and legally formal. Rationalism has led to the doctrine of the works of superarogation, established a balance of duties and merits between God and man, weighing in the scales sins and prayers, trespasses and deeds of expiation; it adopted the idea of transferring one person's debts or credits to another and legalized the exchange of assumed merits; in short, it introduced into the sanctuary of faith the mechanism of a banking house</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=History+of+Russian+Philosophy&amp;rft.pages=87&amp;rft.isbn=978-0-8236-8074-0&amp;rft.aulast=Lossky&amp;rft.aufirst=Nikolai&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEast%E2%80%93West+Schism" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-241"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-241">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">McPartlan, Paul (2000). <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=tSiha9BMxEQC&amp;pg=PR15"><i>Sacrament of Salvation</i></a>. Continuum International. p.&#160;xv. <a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-0-56729299-5" title="Special:BookSources/978-0-56729299-5"><bdi>978-0-56729299-5</bdi></a>.</cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=Sacrament+of+Salvation&amp;rft.pages=xv&amp;rft.pub=Continuum+International&amp;rft.date=2000&amp;rft.isbn=978-0-56729299-5&amp;rft.aulast=McPartlan&amp;rft.aufirst=Paul&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3DtSiha9BMxEQC%26pg%3DPR15&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEast%E2%80%93West+Schism" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>

<li id="cite_note-244"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-244">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">Gaillardetz, Richard R. <li id="cite_note-Cleenewerck2008.p22-245"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Cleenewerck2008.p22_245-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">Cleenewerck, Laurent (1 January 2008). <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=oeKOUb6OcG4C&amp;pg=PA155"><i>His Broken Body: Understanding and Healing the Schism Between the Roman Catholic and Eastern Orthodox Churches</i></a>. Euclid University Press. p.&#160;22. <a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-0-615-18361-9" title="Special:BookSources/978-0-615-18361-9"><bdi>978-0-615-18361-9</bdi></a>. <q>It is my contention in this book, not as a pioneer but as a follower of the great proponents of Eucharistic theology, that the catholic Church is fundamentally the local Eucharistic assembly, gathered around its bishop. Thus, the "Church of God which is at Ephesus or Corinth' is the "whole Church" and the "catholic Church.</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=His+Broken+Body%3A+Understanding+and+Healing+the+Schism+Between+the+Roman+Catholic+and+Eastern+Orthodox+Churches&amp;rft.pages=22&amp;rft.pub=Euclid+University+Press&amp;rft.date=2008-01-01&amp;rft.isbn=978-0-615-18361-9&amp;rft.aulast=Cleenewerck&amp;rft.aufirst=Laurent&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3DoeKOUb6OcG4C%26pg%3DPA155&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEast%E2%80%93West+Schism" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/> <sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Self-published_sources" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability"><span title="This reference citation appears to be to a self-published source. <li id="cite_note-249"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-249">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a href="/wiki/Kallistos_Ware" title="Kallistos Ware">Ware, Kallistos</a> (1995). <i>The Orthodox Church London</i>. St. Vladimir's Seminary Press. <a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-0-913836-58-3" title="Special:BookSources/978-0-913836-58-3"><bdi>978-0-913836-58-3</bdi></a>. <q>as can be seen in the words of 12th century Archbishop <a href="/wiki/Nicetas_of_Nicomedia" title="Nicetas of Nicomedia">Nicetas of Nicomedia</a>: "My dearest brother, we do not deny to the Roman Church the primacy among the five sister patriarchates and we recognize her right to the most honorable seat at the Ecumenical Council. But she has separated herself from us by her own deeds when through pride she assumed a monarchy which does not belong to her office… How shall we accept decrees from her that have been issued without consulting us and even without our knowledge? If the Roman pontiff seated on the lofty throne of his glory wished to thunder at us and, so to speak, hurl his mandates at us from on high and if he wishes to judge us and even to rule us and our churches, not by taking counsel with us but at his own arbitrary pleasure what kind of brotherhood, or even what kind of parenthood can this be? We should be the slaves not the sons, of such a church and the Roman see would not be the pious mother of sons but a hard and imperious mistress of slaves.</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=The+Orthodox+Church+London&amp;rft.pub=St.+Vladimir%27s+Seminary+Press&amp;rft.date=1995&amp;rft.isbn=978-0-913836-58-3&amp;rft.aulast=Ware&amp;rft.aufirst=Kallistos&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEast%E2%80%93West+Schism" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>

<li id="cite_note-250"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-250">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">In 1995, John Paul II wrote: "With the power and the authority without which such an office would be illusory, the Bishop of Rome must ensure the communion of all the Churches." He invited "Church leaders and their theologians to examine with me in a patient and fraternal dialogue on this subject, a dialogue in which, leaving useless controversies behind, we could listen to one another, keeping before us only the will of Christ for his Church and allowing ourselves to be deeply moved by his plea 'that they may all be one ... so that the world may believe that you have sent me' (<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.vatican.va/edocs/ENG0221/__PT.HTM">Encyclical <i>Ut unum sint</i></a> section 96). The <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://orthodoxeurope.org/page/14/130.aspx#2">Ravenna document</a> of 13 October 2007 is one response to this invitation.<cite class="citation web"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20081226130223/http://www.vatican.va/edocs/ENG0221/__PT.HTM">"Archived copy"</a>. <li id="cite_note-256"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-256">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite id="CITEREFII_Vatican_council" class="citation">II Vatican council, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20130306113628/http://www.vatican.va/archive/hist_councils/ii_vatican_council/documents/vat-ii_decree_19641121_unitatis-redintegratio_en.html"><i>Unitatis Redintegratio</i></a>, Rome, IT: The Vatican, n. 17, archived from <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.vatican.va/archive/hist_councils/ii_vatican_council/documents/vat-ii_decree_19641121_unitatis-redintegratio_en.html">the original</a> on 6 March 2013</cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=Unitatis+Redintegratio&amp;rft.place=Rome%2C+IT&amp;rft.pages=n.+17&amp;rft.pub=The+Vatican&amp;rft.au=II+Vatican+council&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.vatican.va%2Farchive%2Fhist_councils%2Fii_vatican_council%2Fdocuments%2Fvat-ii_decree_19641121_unitatis-redintegratio_en.html&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEast%E2%80%93West+Schism" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>

<li id="cite_note-257"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-257">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">Pomazansky, Michael. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.intratext.com/IXT/ENG0824/_P14.HTM"><i>Orthodox Dogmatic Theology</i></a>. <q>The ancient Orthodox teaching of the personal attributes of the Father, Son and Holy Spirit was distorted in the Latin Church by the creation of a teaching of the procession, outside of time and from all eternity, of the Holy Spirit from the Father and the Son – the Filioque. The idea that the Holy Spirit proceeds from the Father and the Son originated in certain expressions of Blessed <a href="/wiki/Augustine" class="mw-redirect" title="Augustine">Augustine</a>. It became established in the West as obligatory in the ninth century, and when Latin missionaries came to the Bulgarians in the middle of the ninth century, the Filioque was in their Symbol of Faith.</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=Orthodox+Dogmatic+Theology&amp;rft.aulast=Pomazansky&amp;rft.aufirst=Michael&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.intratext.com%2FIXT%2FENG0824%2F_P14.HTM&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEast%E2%80%93West+Schism" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-258"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-258">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation web">Romanides, John S. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.romanity.org/htm/rom.18.en.augustine_unknowingly_rejects_the_doctrine.01.htm">"Part I: Augustine's Teachings Which Were Condemned As Those of Barlaam the Calabrian by the Ninth Ecumenical Council of 1351"</a>. <q>Augustine unknowingly rejects the doctrine of the ecumenical councils concerning the Old Testament Lord of glory incarnate and his Vatican and Protestant followers do the same</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Part+I%3A+Augustine%27s+Teachings+Which+Were+Condemned+As+Those+of+Barlaam+the+Calabrian+by+the+Ninth+Ecumenical+Council+of+1351&amp;rft.aulast=Romanides&amp;rft.aufirst=John+S.&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.romanity.org%2Fhtm%2From.18.en.augustine_unknowingly_rejects_the_doctrine.01.htm&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEast%E2%80%93West+Schism" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-259"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-259">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation web">Romanides, John S. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20090729230350/http://www.geocities.com/trvalentine/orthodox/romanides_filioque.html">"Filioque"</a>. Archived from <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.geocities.com/trvalentine/orthodox/romanides_filioque.html">the original</a> on 29 July 2009. <q>The pretext of the Filioque controversy was the Frankish acceptance of Augustine as the key to understanding the theology of the First and Second Ecumenical Synods.</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Filioque&amp;rft.aulast=Romanides&amp;rft.aufirst=John+S.&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.geocities.com%2Ftrvalentine%2Forthodox%2Fromanides_filioque.html&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEast%E2%80%93West+Schism" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-260"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-260">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation web">Romanides, John S. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20090729230350/http://www.geocities.com/trvalentine/orthodox/romanides_filioque.html">"Filioque"</a>. Archived from <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.geocities.com/trvalentine/orthodox/romanides_filioque.html">the original</a> on 29 July 2009. <q>During the ensuing centuries long course of the controversy, the Franks not only forced the Patristic tradition into an Augustinian mold, but they confused Augustine's Trinitarian terminology with that of the Father's of the First and Second Ecumenical Synods. This is nowhere so evident as in the Latin handling of Maximos the Confessor's description, composed in 650, of the West Roman Orthodox Filioque at the Council of Florence (1438–42). The East Romans hesitated to present Maximos' letter to Marinos about this West Roman Orthodox Filioque because the letter did not survive in its complete form.</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Filioque&amp;rft.aulast=Romanides&amp;rft.aufirst=John+S.&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.geocities.com%2Ftrvalentine%2Forthodox%2Fromanides_filioque.html&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEast%E2%80%93West+Schism" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-261"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-261">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">Romanides, John S. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.romanity.org/htm/rom.03.en.franks_romans_feudalism_and_doctrine.02.htm"><i>Franks, Romans, Feudalism, and Doctrine – Part 2. Empirical Theology versus Speculative Theology -Empirical Theology</i></a>. <q>A basic characteristic of the Frankish scholastic method, mislead by Augustinian Platonism and Thomistic Aristotelianism, had been its naïve confidence in the objective existence of things rationally speculated about. By following Augustine, the Franks substituted the patristic concern for spiritual observation, (which they had found firmly established in Gaul when they first conquered the area) with a fascination for metaphysics. They did not suspect that such speculations had foundations neither in created nor in spiritual reality.</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=Franks%2C+Romans%2C+Feudalism%2C+and+Doctrine+%E2%80%93+Part+2.+Empirical+Theology+versus+Speculative+Theology+-Empirical+Theology&amp;rft.aulast=Romanides&amp;rft.aufirst=John+S.&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.romanity.org%2Fhtm%2From.03.en.franks_romans_feudalism_and_doctrine.02.htm&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEast%E2%80%93West+Schism" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>
</li>

<li id="cite_note-273"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-273">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">Lossky, Vladimir (1997). <i>The Mystical Theology of the Eastern Church</i>. SVS Press. <a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0-913836-31-1" title="Special:BookSources/0-913836-31-1"><bdi>0-913836-31-1</bdi></a>.</cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=The+Mystical+Theology+of+the+Eastern+Church&amp;rft.pub=SVS+Press&amp;rft.date=1997&amp;rft.isbn=0-913836-31-1&amp;rft.aulast=Lossky&amp;rft.aufirst=Vladimir&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEast%E2%80%93West+Schism" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>

<li id="cite_note-274"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-274">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation web">Pomazansky, Michael. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.intratext.com/IXT/ENG0824/_P14.HTM">"On the procession of the Holy Spirit"</a>. <q>Oneness of Essence, and it is absolutely essential to distinguish this from another dogma, the dogma of the begetting and the procession, in which, as the Holy Fathers express it, is shown the Cause of the existence of the Son and the Spirit. All of the Eastern Fathers acknowledge that the Father is monos aitios, the sole Cause" of the Son and the Spirit. Orthodox Dogmatic Theology</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=On+the+procession+of+the+Holy+Spirit&amp;rft.aulast=Pomazansky&amp;rft.aufirst=Michael&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.intratext.com%2FIXT%2FENG0824%2F_P14.HTM&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEast%E2%80%93West+Schism" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>

<li id="cite_note-275"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-275">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">"The Filioque controversy which has separated us for so many centuries is more than a mere technicality, but it is not insoluble. Qualifying the firm position taken when I wrote The Orthodox Church twenty years ago, I now believe, after further study, that the problem is more in the area of semantics than in any basic doctrinal differences." (Bishop Kallistos Ware, Diakonia, quoted from Elias Zoghby's A Voice from the Byzantine East, p. 43).</span>

<li id="cite_note-276"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-276">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">In the Introduction p. 21 "We have become different men" The Mystical Theology of the Eastern Church, by Vladimir Lossky, SVS Press, 1997. (<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/><a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0-913836-31-1" title="Special:BookSources/0-913836-31-1">0-913836-31-1</a>) James Clarke &amp; Co. Ltd., 1991. (<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/><a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0-227-67919-9" title="Special:BookSources/0-227-67919-9">0-227-67919-9</a>)</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-277"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-277">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation web">Romanides, John S. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.romanity.org/htm/rom.03.en.franks_romans_feudalism_and_doctrine.02.htm">"Franks, Romans, Feudalism, and Doctrine – Part 2. Empirical Theology versus Speculative Theology -Empirical Theology"</a>. <q>A basic characteristic of the Frankish scholastic method, misled by Augustinian Platonism and Thomistic Aristotelianism, had been its naïve confidence in the objective existence of things rationally speculated about. By following Augustine, the Franks substituted the patristic concern for spiritual observation, (which they had found firmly established in Gaul when they first conquered the area) with a fascination for metaphysics. They did not suspect that such speculations had foundations neither in created nor in spiritual reality. No one would today accept as true what is not empirically observable, or at least verifiable by inference, from an attested effect. So it is with patristic theology. Dialectical speculation about God and the Incarnation as such are rejected. Only those things which can be tested by the experience of the grace of God in the heart are to be accepted. "Be not carried about by divers and strange teachings. For it is good that the heart be confirmed by grace," a passage from Hebrews 13.9, quoted by the Fathers to this effect.</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Franks%2C+Romans%2C+Feudalism%2C+and+Doctrine+%E2%80%93+Part+2.+Empirical+Theology+versus+Speculative+Theology+-Empirical+Theology&amp;rft.aulast=Romanides&amp;rft.aufirst=John+S.&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.romanity.org%2Fhtm%2From.03.en.franks_romans_feudalism_and_doctrine.02.htm&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEast%E2%80%93West+Schism" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-278"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-278">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation web">Metropolitan Hierotheos of Nafpaktos. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20090105041142/http://www.pelagia.org/htm/b02.en.orthodox_psychotherapy.06.htm">"Knowledge of God according to St. Gregory Palamas"</a>. Archived from <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.pelagia.org/htm/b02.en.orthodox_psychotherapy.06.htm#2k">the original</a> on 5 January 2009. <q>As I have indicated, <a href="/wiki/Barlaam_of_Seminara" title="Barlaam of Seminara">Barlaam</a> insisted that knowledge of God depends not on vision of God but on one's understanding. He said that we can acquire knowledge of God through philosophy, and therefore he considered the prophets and apostles who saw the <a href="/wiki/Tabor_light" class="mw-redirect" title="Tabor light">uncreated light</a>, to be below the philosophers. He called the uncreated light sensory, created, and "inferior to our understanding". However, St. Gregory Palamas, a bearer of the Tradition and a man of revelation, supported the opposite view. In his theology he presented the teaching of the Church that uncreated light, that is, the <a href="/wiki/Theoria" class="mw-redirect" title="Theoria">vision of God</a>, is not simply a symbolic vision, nor sensory and created, nor inferior to understanding, but it is deification. Through deification man is deemed worthy of seeing God. And this deification is not an abstract state, but a union of man with God. That is to say, the man who beholds the uncreated light sees it because he is united with God. He sees it with his inner eyes, and also with his bodily eyes, which, however, have been altered by God's action. Consequently theoria is <a href="/wiki/Theosis_(Eastern_Orthodox_theology)" class="mw-redirect" title="Theosis (Eastern Orthodox theology)">union with God</a>. And this union is knowledge of God. At this time one is granted knowledge of God, which is above human knowledge and above the senses.</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Knowledge+of+God+according+to+St.+Gregory+Palamas&amp;rft.au=Metropolitan+Hierotheos+of+Nafpaktos&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.pelagia.org%2Fhtm%2Fb02.en.orthodox_psychotherapy.06.htm%232k&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEast%E2%80%93West+Schism" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-279"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-279">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">Pomazansky, Michael. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.intratext.com/IXT/ENG0824/_P2N.HTM"><i>Orthodox Dogmatic Theology: A Concise Exposition Protopresbyter Appendices New currents in Russian philosophico-theological thought Philosophy and Theology</i></a>.</cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=Orthodox+Dogmatic+Theology%3A+A+Concise+Exposition+Protopresbyter+Appendices+New+currents+in+Russian+philosophico-theological+thought+Philosophy+and+Theology&amp;rft.aulast=Pomazansky&amp;rft.aufirst=Michael&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.intratext.com%2FIXT%2FENG0824%2F_P2N.HTM&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEast%E2%80%93West+Schism" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-280"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-280">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">"Roman Catholicism rationalizes even the sacrament of the Eucharist: it interprets spiritual action as purely material and debases the sacrament to such an extent that it becomes in its view a kind of atomistic miracle. The Orthodox Church has no metaphysical theory of Transsubstantiation, and there is no need of such a theory. Christ is the Lord of the elements and it is in His power to do so that 'every thing, without in the least changing its physical substance' could become His Body. Christ's Body in the Eucharist is not physical flesh." <li id="cite_note-Neuro-289"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-Neuro_289-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-Neuro_289-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">"Augustine claims that all humans have sinned in Adam. The <a href="/wiki/Council_of_Orange_(529)" title="Council of Orange (529)">Council</a>, however, interprets Rom. 5:12 as saying that, 'By one man sin entered the world, and by sin death, and thus to all men [death] passed, in which all have sinned.' In other words all sin because of the spiritual death which each one suffers by not being in communion with the glory of God": Romanides</span>

<li id="cite_note-301"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-301">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.ocf.org/OrthodoxPage/reading/ortho_cath.html">[3]</a> "from '&#x27;the first instant of her conception, the Blessed Virgin Mary was, by a most singular grace and privilege of Almighty God, and in view of the merits of Jesus Christ, the Redeemer of the human race, preserved from all stain of Original Sin. It is a doctrine revealed by God, and therefore to be firmly and steadfastly believed by all the faithful'&#x27; (from the '&#x27;Bull Ineffabilis Deus'&#x27;)." WHAT ARE THE DIFFERENCES BETWEEN ORTHODOXY AND ROMAN CATHOLICISM? By Father Michael Azkoul.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-302"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-302">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.orthodoxinfo.com/inquirers/theotokos.aspx">[4]</a> "However, we do believe that the Virgin Mary is an image, as St. Maximos the Confessor says, of the Christian goal of becoming Christ-like, of '&#x27;theosis'&#x27;. Just as the Theotokos gave birth to Christ in a bodily way, so we must, St. Maximos tells us, give birth to Christ in an unbodily or spiritual way. In so doing, we imitate her practical spiritual life, including the purity and humility by which she formed her free will into perfect obedience to the Will of God.", "we cannot lose sight of the importance of free will in the development and expression of her rich personality." An Orthodox View of the Virgin Mary.</span>

<li id="cite_note-318"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-318">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite id="CITEREFLossky1976" class="citation">Lossky, V (January 1976), <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=dxqvWwPSCSwC#PPA234,M1"><i>The Mystical Theology of the Eastern Church</i></a>, p.&#160;234, <a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-0-913836-31-6" title="Special:BookSources/978-0-913836-31-6"><bdi>978-0-913836-31-6</bdi></a>, <q>Hell is not so much a place where God imprisons man as a place where man, by misusing his free will, chooses to imprison himself. And even in hell the wicked are not deprived of the love of God, but by their own choice they experience as suffering what the saints experience as joy. 'The love of God will be an intolerable torment for those who have not acquired it within themselves</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=The+Mystical+Theology+of+the+Eastern+Church&amp;rft.pages=234&amp;rft.date=1976-01&amp;rft.isbn=978-0-913836-31-6&amp;rft.aulast=Lossky&amp;rft.aufirst=V&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3DdxqvWwPSCSwC%23PPA234%2CM1&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEast%E2%80%93West+Schism" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>
